  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_a90dfe7b-9df5-46c3-a4a8-afd33391b35d'
      });

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2319478229" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6374223623770801640">Op de babyshower voor onze dochter, kregen mijn man en ik van een vriendin het voorleesboek van Jip en Janneke. <br/>Dit boek telt 347 pagina's puur leesplezier.<br/>Onze dochter is nu 19 weken oud en wanneer ik het boek pak begint ze al te lachen die slimmerik. En jong als ze is, bij elk verhaaltje lacht ze nog harder dan bij het vorige verhaaltje.<br/>Annie M.G. Schmidt neemt je door de ogen van Jip en Janneke mee door allerlei gebeurtenissen en avonturen die ze beleven. <br/>Zo gaan Jip en Janneke naar de dieren</span>
  <span id="freeText6374223623770801640" style="display:none">Op de babyshower voor onze dochter, kregen mijn man en ik van een vriendin het voorleesboek van Jip en Janneke. <br />Dit boek telt 347 pagina's puur leesplezier.<br />Onze dochter is nu 19 weken oud en wanneer ik het boek pak begint ze al te lachen die slimmerik. En jong als ze is, bij elk verhaaltje lacht ze nog harder dan bij het vorige verhaaltje.<br />Annie M.G. Schmidt neemt je door de ogen van Jip en Janneke mee door allerlei gebeurtenissen en avonturen die ze beleven. <br />Zo gaan Jip en Janneke naar de dierentuin, uit logeren, achter Sinterklaas aan, stelen ze een kerstboom en halen ze allemaal kattenkwaad uit.<br /><br />Ik raad iedere ouder aan dit boek in huis te hebben. De kleintjes vinden dit boek geweldig.</span>
  <a data-text-id="6374223623770801640" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer12411869935656032302">Als kind vond ik het geweldig om een verhaaltje uit het Jip en Janneke boek te lezen (of voor te laten lezen).   <span id="freeText12411869935656032302" style="display:none">Als kind vond ik het geweldig om een verhaaltje uit het Jip en Janneke boek te lezen (of voor te laten lezen). De twee maken allerlei leuke en gekke, maar juist ook alledaagse dingen mee. Veel van deze verhalen kan ik mij nu nog steeds herinneren en ook heb ik vroeger een van de verhalen mogen opdragen op het podium bij de week afsluiting als Janneke! (Elke vrijdag werden er op de basisschool toneelstukjes opgevoerd voor alle ouders en kinderen van de school). <br /><br />-----<br />Omschrijving (Bol.com):<br /><br />Jip en Janneke zijn twee kleuters (buurkinderen) die heel gewone, dagelijkse dingen meemaken. Elk verhaaltje in deze verzamelbundel is een afgerond geheel en speelt zich af in de kleuterwereld; alles is heel herkenbaar. Een geweldig voorleesboek voor peuters en kleuters, mede door de vele leuke zwart-witte en enkele paginagrote tekeningen in frisse kleuren. Achterin zijn een register naar onderwerp en een inhoudsopgave opgenomen. Het onderwerpenregister is niet volledig, maar bevat wel onderwerpen die de belangstelling hebben, zoals feestdagen, familie en dieren. Kloeke uitgave in tweekolommendruk. De opmaak is zodanig dat tekst en bijbehorende tekeningen goed bij elkaar staan. Vanaf ca. 3 jaar.</span>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer396356224" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7947637338002570962">Volledige uitgave van de ultrakorte verhaaltjes (1953-1960) over de buurkinderen Jip en Janneke. Sommige verhaaltjes zijn duidelijk gedateerd (de melkman, de schilleboer), maar ze zijn allen zeer herkenbaar en nog steeds fris. Ze beschrijven precies hoe je vroeger toen je klein was dingen kon ervaren, en halen die vroege herinneringen met gemak terug, zelfs als je dacht dat je ze vergeten was. Grote klasse!<br/></span>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer3208103336004393913">Dit is het boek dat mijn ouders elke avond aan mij voorlazen als kind. Nog steeds kan ik genieten van de verhaaltjes van Jip en Janneke. Het boek is versiert met illustraties van Fiep van Westendorp, het mooi aan dit boek is dat Jip en Janneke beide altijd in zwart/wit zijn afgebeeld. Het zijn kindertjes die overal ter wereld kunnen wonen.</span>

          </span>

<div id="review_266139999" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/266139999" />
    <a title="Mirjam" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/7104014-mirjam"><img alt="Mirjam" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1529171720p2/7104014.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/266139999?book_show_action=true">Jan 22, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Mirjam" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Mirjam" href="/user/show/7104014-mirjam">Mirjam</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Hardcover 9789045106656" href="/book/show/8417331-jip-and-janneke---two-kids-from-holland">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer266139999" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5110017247342002614">WAIT: This isn't the right book. The one we read is called just "Jip and Janneke" -- not "Jip and Janneke; Two kids from Holland." That one's cool too; we have it, but it's not the story collection the other is.<br/><br/>Anyway ...<br/><br/>Read the whole just "Jip and Janneke" to my daughter (who is sick and voiceless) this morning ... and she said -- whispered, barely -- that the stories made her "feel better." <br/><br/>Five stars for that alone.<br/><br/>Five stars also for being able to share with my 4-year-old girl (in English) </span>
  <span id="freeText5110017247342002614" style="display:none">WAIT: This isn't the right book. The one we read is called just "Jip and Janneke" -- not "Jip and Janneke; Two kids from Holland." That one's cool too; we have it, but it's not the story collection the other is.<br /><br />Anyway ...<br /><br />Read the whole just "Jip and Janneke" to my daughter (who is sick and voiceless) this morning ... and she said -- whispered, barely -- that the stories made her "feel better." <br /><br />Five stars for that alone.<br /><br />Five stars also for being able to share with my 4-year-old girl (in English) the stories my Mommy read to me (in Dutch) when I was her age!<br /><br />And that Jip ("Yip," it's pronounced, y'all), "Jip's so silly."<br /><br />I can't say that I precisely remember any of these short stories -- think authentically silly, brilliant two-minute fiction about two little 4/5-year-old buddies, sometimes laugh-out-loud funny (even if you have no voice) and sometimes downright poignant, each one so good you can't help but want to read the next one for another hit of the magic.<br /><br />But I definitely remember the characters and, weirdly, I recognized a lot of myself and my writing in the writing of these perfect little ditties. <br /><br />These are the style of stories I still love, the rhythm, the direction, the realness. These ain't Dora stories where nothing is plausible but, worse, the fantasy is ridiculous and lazy. Here everything that happens on these pages could, or, well, probably DID happen, perhaps thousands of times around the world to you and me and yours and mine ... A talented Annie M.G. Schmidt probably simply had the good idea to chronicle her kid's play.<br /><br />And it worked! We're let into these kids' world of believable make believe, and that's the beauty of it: Delivering the magic of the ordinary, the wonder of the world around a 4-year old, when uncles with beards are scary and cool, aunties with cars (hey, this is Holland in the '70s) are even cooler and chocolate bars, oh chocolate bars! <br /><br />And the types of payoffs each story provides! "And they play marbles." "And that's fast, too." " 'Well,' says Mother, 'you asked for it.' " -- one-line conclusions that tie everything up satisfyingly, stylishly, funnily ... <br /><br />And it all is so right on and ... me. Could I have been conditioned to love this type of story-telling, to want to tell stories like this because I was exposed to these stories way back when I was 4?<br /><br />Our favorite story, I think, judging by the silent and not-so-silent guffawing that took place: "Bear falls out of the plane"<br /><br />And I just have to give anyone not reading this -- 'cause who's reading this? -- a sample:<br /><br /><i>Jip has been to the airport with his father. He saw planes from very close by. 'They're ever bigger than our house,' he tells Janneke. 'They're as big as from here to the church.'<br /><br />'They can't be,' Janneke says. 'In the sky they're just teensy-weensy.'<br /><br />'It's still true,' Jip says. 'And there are people inside. And the pilot sits at the front. Shall we play aeroplanes?'<br /><br />They line up some chairs. And the piano stool is the steering wheel. Janneke is a lady who's going on the plane, and Dolly-dee and Bear are her children. Jip gets to be the pilot.<br /><br />'Will you drive carefully, pilot?' asks the lady.<br /><br />'Drive?' says the pilot. 'We're not driving, we're flying.'<br /><br />'Will you make sure my children don't fall out of the plane?' the lady asks again.<br /><br />'I'll make sure they don't,' says the pilot. 'And here's a parachute in case they do. Just tie it on.'<br /><br />Off they go. Brrr-br-brrr-brrrr... the plane takes off, up into the sky.<br /><br />'Oh no,' the lady shouts, 'my children are getting so dizzy.'<br /><br />'Too late now,' the pilot says. 'We're already a hundred feet up. We're already in Africa.'<br /><br />'Oh no,' the lady shouts again. 'One of my children just fell out of the window.'<br /><br />'Did she have a parachute?' the pilot shouts back.<br /><br />'Yes.'<br /><br />'Then she's fine. We'll keep going.'<br /><br />'The other one just fell out of the window as well,' the lady shouts.<br /><br />'Did he have a parachute?'<br /><br />'No, we only had one.'<br /><br />'Then he's dead,' the pilot says.<br /><br />'Oh, oh!' the lady screams. 'We have to land right away.'<br /><br />Brrr-brrr-brrr... the plane goes back down to the ground.<br /><br />What a relief! Both children are alive and kicking, Bear without a parachute and Dolly-Dee with a parachute.<br /><br />'Goodbye, pilot,' says the lady. 'Thank you very much for the drive.'<br /><br />'Goodbye, madam,' says the pilot.</i><br /><br /><br />.... and that's what I mean. You don't get away with writing a children's story about children falling out of airplanes and maybe dying unless you've convinced your readers that it's the kids telling the story, unless you KNOW it is the kids telling the stories. </span>
  <a data-text-id="5110017247342002614" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_472099675" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/472099675" />

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/472099675?book_show_action=true">Dec 07, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Derek Cooke" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Derek Cooke" href="/user/show/12334410-derek-cooke">Derek Cooke</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Hardcover 9789045106656" href="/book/show/8417331-jip-and-janneke---two-kids-from-holland">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer472099675" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer708919350238454761">This is a wonderful story as told by Jip and Janneke. The two silhouettes spend the entire book taking you, the reader, on a trip across their country of Holland. The book is written as if Jip and Janneke were personally taking you around the country, showing you the absolute best things about Holland. They start out with the basics and talk about the King and Queen of Holland as well as the canals, windmills and tulips that Holland is known for. The story is then broken down in to the four seas</span>
  <span id="freeText708919350238454761" style="display:none">This is a wonderful story as told by Jip and Janneke. The two silhouettes spend the entire book taking you, the reader, on a trip across their country of Holland. The book is written as if Jip and Janneke were personally taking you around the country, showing you the absolute best things about Holland. They start out with the basics and talk about the King and Queen of Holland as well as the canals, windmills and tulips that Holland is known for. The story is then broken down in to the four seasons and what the Dutch do during these times. Spring was mostly dedicated to Easter and how the children decorate eggs. Summer is all about ice cream, trips and hot lazy days. Autumn is the decline of weather and the fall fair. Winter brings snow and St Nicholas along with Christmas. The book ends kind of abruptly after the winter section.</span>
  <a data-text-id="708919350238454761" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('sD++CB1AvwE1weC5bUe/uAOGy+VfSdb7nw6gSXudokX1uqVEOaAiHuOY7xB96pHvOPYZEfuR/lvAYZJ8dSuUhA==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('rm3kQT1ZJFlGxfqR6eRJqv/+Y5CAKFoe1iKQHCfk31Dr6P8NGbm5RpCc9Tj5SWf9xI6xZCTwcr6JTaIpKVLpkQ==')})
  }

De ministers geven Stach zeven bijna onuitvoerbare opdrachten, waarop al velen voor hem hun kracht beproefd hebben. Maar Stach is niet bang. <div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer17572391707504887728">Anna Maria Geertruida Schmidt was a Dutch writer.<br/><br/>Although she wrote a variety of poems, songs, books, plays, musicals, and radio- en television drama, she is known best for her children's literature, for which she received the Hans Christian Andersen Award in 1988. She committed suicide a day after her 84th birthday and was buried in Amsterdam.<br/></span>
